          <script>
           $("#category-search-form .search-button").click(function() {
    var zip_field;
    zip_field = $("#search_city");
    if (zip_field.val() === '' || zip_field.val() === zip_field.attr('placeholder')) {
      $("#where_field").append('<div class="highlighted-bg error"><span>Where are you looking?</span></div>').focus();
      $("#where_field input[type='text']").addClass('msg-error');
      return false;
    }
  });
  
  
  $('.trigger-biz-js').on('click', function(){
    $('.trigger-biz-element').toggleClass('off on');
    $('.hero-where-field').toggleClass('single-input');
    $('#search_city').toggleClass('border-left');
  })
  
  $(".switch-search").switchSearch();
  $("[data-action='setSubCategoryId']").subcategoryChooser();
  $(document).ready(function(){
    $("#search_city").keypress(function(){
      $(".unmappable-container").animate({
          opacity: 0
        }, 800, function() {
          return $(this).remove();
        });
    });
    // Prevents highlighted field from disappearing
    $("#search_city").mouseup(function(e) {return false; });
  
    hideMagic = function(){
      setTimeout(function(){
        $('#magic').remove();
      },'300');
    }
  
    toggleSubCats = function() {
  
      var theWidth = $('.hero-input-container').width();
      var scPos = $('#ChooseSubCategorySelect').position();
      var theDiff = Math.round((scPos.left)) + (theWidth/2);
      var catChooserWidth= Math.round(($('#category_chooser').width())/2);
      var centerThis = (theDiff - catChooserWidth);
      var winWidth = $(window).width();
  
      if (825 > winWidth) {
        $('#category_chooser').css('width', '100%');
      } else {
        $('#category_chooser').css('width', '825px');
      }
  
      $('#category_chooser').css('left', centerThis);
  
      if ($('#category_chooser').is(':visible')){
        $('#category_chooser').slideUp({
            duration: '500',
            easing: 'easeInBack'
        });
      } else if ($('#category_chooser').is(':hidden')) {
        $('#category_chooser').slideDown({
          duration: '1000',
          easing: 'easeOutBack'
        });
      }
      $('#magic').click(function(){
        $('#category_chooser').slideUp({
            duration: '500',
            easing: 'easeInBack'
        });
        hideMagic();
      });
    }
  
    $('#ChooseSubCategoryText').click(function(){
      $('body').append('<div id="magic"><div id="magic_inner">&nbsp;</div></div>');
      toggleSubCats();
    });
  
    $('.subcat-selector').click(function(){
      toggleSubCats();
      hideMagic();
    });
  });
          </script>
